RUS_setup_senate_duma_conflict_variables = {
	set_variable = { RUS_senate_authority = 25 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_senate_pop_support = party_popularity@social_conservative }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_senate_pop_support = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_senate_pop_support = party_popularity@market_liberal }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_senate_pop_support = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_senate_pop_support = 100 }
		
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = popular_support }
	set_variable = { RUS_senate_pol_power = temp1 }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_senate_pol_power = temp2 }
	divide_variable = { RUS_senate_pol_power = 2 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_senate_pol_power = 100 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_duma_authority = 35 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = party_popularity@radical_socialist }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = party_popularity@syndicalist }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = party_popularity@social_democrat }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = party_popularity@social_liberal }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = party_popularity@national_populist }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_duma_pop_support = 100 }
		
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = popular_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = 2 }
	set_variable = { RUS_duma_pol_power = temp1 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_duma_pol_power = 100 }
	
}
	
RUS_calculate_government_variables = {
	RUS_popular_support_recalc = yes
	RUS_army_support_recalc = yes
	RUS_average_support_recalc = yes
}
RUS_average_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = popular_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = 2 }
	set_variable = { average_pop_arm_support = temp1 }
}
RUS_popular_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@ruling_party }
	set_temp_variable = { temp3 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp3 = modifier@consumer_goods_factor }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp3 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS.stability }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp2 < 0.5 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { temp1 = additional_popular_support }
	set_variable = { popular_support = temp1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = popular_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
}
RUS_army_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@ruling_party }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS.war_support }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp2 < 0.5 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_dealt_with_army_mutiny }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { temp1 = additional_army_support }
	set_variable = { army_support = temp1 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	set_variable = { opposite_army_support = temp1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = army_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
}
RUS_clear_all_coalitions = {
	clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
	clr_country_flag = psr_coalition
	clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
	clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
	clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
	clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
	clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
	end_coalition = yes
}
RUS_setup_initial_senate = {
	set_variable = { plsr_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_total_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { psr_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators = 17 }
	set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 6 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_total_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_total_regional_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 6 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_senators = 4 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_regional_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { vns_total_senators = 37 }
	set_variable = { vns_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { vns_presidential_senators = 20 }
	set_variable = { ep_total_senators = 5 }
	set_variable = { ep_total_regional_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { ep_presidential_senators = 16 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_total_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_total_regional_senators = 5 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { independent_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { independent_total_regional_senators = 22 }
	set_variable = { independent_presidential_senators = 0 }
	final_senators_recalc = yes
	calculate_half_senate = yes
	calculate_two_thirds_senate = yes
	calculate_half_duma = yes
	calculate_two_thirds_duma = yes
}
calculate_half_senate = {
	set_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = senate_total }
	divide_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = 1 }
}
calculate_two_thirds_senate = {
	set_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = senate_total }
	multiply_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 2}
	divide_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 1 }
}
calculate_half_duma = {
	set_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = mp_total }
	divide_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = half_duma_plus_one
}
calculate_two_thirds_duma = {
	set_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = mp_total }
	multiply_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 2}
	divide_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = two_thirds_duma_plus_one
}

RUS_setup_initial_state_popularities = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_owned_by = RUS
					is_core_of = RUS
				}
				is_owned_by = TRM
				is_owned_by = FIN
				is_owned_by = ALO
				is_owned_by = UKR
				is_owned_by = WHR
				is_owned_by = KUB
				is_owned_by = DKB
				is_owned_by = KLY
				is_owned_by = GEO
				is_owned_by = ARM
				is_owned_by = POL
				is_owned_by = LIT
				is_owned_by = BAT
				is_owned_by = GAL
				is_owned_by = ROM
				is_owned_by = MTR
				is_owned_by = AZE
				is_owned_by = KYR
				is_owned_by = TRK
				is_owned_by = UZB
				is_owned_by = MON
			}
		}
		RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes
		set_variable = { RUS_state_general_turnout = 0.7 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_senate_turnout = 0.3 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout = 0.2 }
		set_variable = { RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout = 1 }
		RUS_clamp_all_state_pop = yes
	}
}
RUS_generate_state_popularities = {
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0 }
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }	
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.4 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.6 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 0 }
	}
	#Adjust for ROVS
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = 0.1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = 0.4 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = 0.25 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = 0.25 }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction }
	}
		
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.5 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.5 }
	
		
	#Defining temporary state pop variables (to be reset by election)
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }
	
	RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = yes
	
}
RUS_adjusted_state_pops = {
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@totalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@social_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = OWNER.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_popularity = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 0 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.07 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.03 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_socdem_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 0.08 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
				NOT = { tag = DKB }
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				OR = {
					tag = TRM
					tag = DKB
				}
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				tag = TRM
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = yes

	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }	
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = NSNP_separated } }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.4 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.6 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 0 }
	}
	
}
RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = {
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }	
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.4 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.6 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0 }
	}
	### VNS Buff ###
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.1 }
	### Minorities ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 215
				state = 216
				state = 401
				state = 236
				state = 1197
				state = 1199
				state = 256
				state = 1193
				state = 399
				state = 397
				state = 651
				state = 1194
				state = 880
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.25 }
	}
	### Oblastniki Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_siberia = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	### South Russia Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 265
				state = 239
				state = 250
				state = 401
				state = 217
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0.15 }
	}
	### PSR & NRPR Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_rrf_state = yes				
				state = 221	
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 248		
				state = 573	
				state = 399
				state = 252
				state = 226
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	### Urban Buff ###
	set_temp_variable = { industrial_popularity = THIS.num_of_factories }
	divide_temp_variable = { industrial_popularity = 75 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = industrial_popularity }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = industrial_popularity }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_state_category = seven
				has_state_category = eight
				has_state_category = nine
				has_state_category = ten
				has_state_category = eleven
				has_state_category = twelve
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 219
				state = 195 
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	### Kuban Region ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = DKB
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.20 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0.35 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = -0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = -0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = KUB
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = -0.35 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = -0.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			state = 235
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.25 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = KLY
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = -0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.35 }
	}
	if = {

			is_core_of = MTR
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.35 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.15 }
	}
	### Transcaucasia ###
	if = {

		}

		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.35 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = ARM
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.3 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.25 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = AZE
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.3 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.3 }
	}
	### Ukraine & Belarus
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = WHR
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = -0.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_core_of = UKR
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.3 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = -0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = -0.1 }

	### Central Asia ###

		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = -0.5 }

#Calculates polling averages - to clear later
RUS_calculate_polling_averages = {
	RUS_clear_polling_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_plsr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_vns_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_ep_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_independent_popularity }

	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_psr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_vns_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_ep_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_independent_temp_pop }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}	
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}	
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop < 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = 0 }
	}
	

	set_variable = { RUS_poll_count_state = state_population_k }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_poll_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop }

	multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_poll_votes = RUS_poll_count_state }
	
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_poll_votes = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_poll_votes = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
	
	
	ROOT = {
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
		
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
		
		divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
		
	}

	log = "[THIS.GetName]: FINAL POLLING RESULTS - PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote])"
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: FINAL POLLING RESULTS - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote]) - EP ([?RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote])"
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: FINAL POLLING RESULTS - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_state_votes])"

}

	clear_variable = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop
	clear_variable = RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop

RUS_get_final_popularities = {
	#Prevents modifiers from stacking endlessly
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_plsr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_vns_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_ep_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_popularity }

	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_psr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_psr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_vns_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_ep_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_temp_pop }
}
RUS_run_senate_election = {
	RUS_clear_senate_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_votes = 0 }
		
	set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_senate_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_state_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		
		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_state_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_state_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_state_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_senate_state_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_psr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_vns_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_ep_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_state_votes = RUS_independent_senate_state_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_senate_votes = RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_senate_votes = RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_senate_votes = RUS_psr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_senate_votes = RUS_vns_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_senate_votes = RUS_ep_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = RUS_nsnp_senate_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_senate_votes = RUS_independent_senate_state_votes }

		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }

		log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_senate_state_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_senate_state_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_senate_state_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_senate_state_votes]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_senate_state_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_senate_state_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_senate_state_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_senate_state_votes]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_senate_state_votes]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_senate_state_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_senate_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = NSNP_separated } }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_plsr_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_nsp_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_psr_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_vns_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_ep_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_nrpr_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_nsnp_senate_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_independent_senate_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_plsr_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_nsp_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_psr_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_lkdp_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_rkdp_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_vns_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_ep_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_nrpr_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_nsnp_senate_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_independent_senate_votes }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_senate_vote = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	
	multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_senate_vote = 100 }

	
	round_variable = RUS_total_senate_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR([?RUS_plsr_senate_votes]) - NSP([?RUS_nsp_senate_votes]) - RSDRP([?RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes]) - PSR([?RUS_psr_senate_votes]) - KDP([?RUS_kdp_senate_votes]) - VNS([?RUS_vns_senate_votes]) - EP([?RUS_ep_senate_votes]) - NRPR([?RUS_nrpr_senate_votes]) - IND([?RUS_independent_senate_votes]) - TOTAL([?RUS_total_senate_votes])"
	parties_senators_recalc = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
}

RUS_run_election = {
	RUS_clear_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }

		log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_state_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_state_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_state_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_state_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_state_votes]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_state_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_state_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_state_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_state_votes]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_state_votes]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_state_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = NSNP_separated } }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_independent_votes }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_popular_front_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { RUS_socialists_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_socialists_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	}
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_votes = RUS_kdp_votes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_votes = RUS_kdp_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
	}
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_kdp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_plsr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_psr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_rkdp_votes }

	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes

		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_votes

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
