	}
	round_variable = RUS_total_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: RSDRP([?RUS_rsdrp_votes]) - PSR([?RUS_psr_votes]) - KDP([?RUS_kdp_votes]) - VNS([?RUS_vns_votes]) - EP([?RUS_ep_votes]) - NRPR([?RUS_nrpr_votes]) - IND([?RUS_independent_votes]) - TOTAL([?RUS_total_votes])"
	parties_mp_recalc = yes
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
}
RUS_run_1941_election = {
	RUS_clear_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = RUS.RUS_starting_states_array
		
		THIS = { RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes }
	}
	
	every_owned_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				rsdrp_in_power = yes
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.15 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				psr_in_power = yes
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.15 }
		}
		
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }

		log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_state_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_state_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_state_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_state_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_state_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_state_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_state_votes]) - EP ([?RUS_ep_state_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_state_votes]) - NSNP ([?RUS_nsnp_state_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: IND ([?RUS_independent_state_votes]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_state_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = NSNP_separated } }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_independent_votes }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_socialists_votes = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rpr_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_rpr_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	}
	
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
		
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_plsr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_psr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_vns_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_ep_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_independent_votes }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	
	multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = 100 }

	
	
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rrdo_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_plsr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rrdo_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_socialists_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_psr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rrdo_votes > RUS_socialists_votes }

	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_rovs_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes

		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes

		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes

	multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_rovs_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = 100 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_plsr_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsp_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_psr_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rsdrp_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_lkdp_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rkdp_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_vns_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_ep_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes > RUS_nsnp_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nrpr_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_plsr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_nsp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_psr_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_rsdrp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_lkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_rkdp_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_vns_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_ep_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_rovs_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes > RUS_nrpr_votes }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsnp_president_victory
	}
	round_variable = RUS_total_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR([?RUS_plsr_votes]) - NSP([?RUS_nsp_votes]) - RSDRP([?RUS_rsdrp_votes]) - PSR([?RUS_psr_votes]) - KDP([?RUS_kdp_votes]) - VNS([?RUS_vns_votes]) - EP([?RUS_ep_votes]) - NRPR([?RUS_nrpr_votes]) - IND([?RUS_independent_votes]) - TOTAL([?RUS_total_votes])"
}

mp_support_calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = plsr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rsdrp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = psr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = lkdp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rkdp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = vns_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = ep_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nrpr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsnp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = independent_mp }
	set_variable = { mp_support = temp1 }
}
senators_support_calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0 }
	set_variable = { plsr_senators = plsr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { nsp_senators = nsp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { psr_senators = psr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_senators = rsdrp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { lkdp_senators = lkdp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { rkdp_senators = rkdp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { vns_senators = vns_final_senators }
	set_variable = { ep_senators = ep_final_senators }
	set_variable = { nrpr_senators = nrpr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { nsnp_senators = nsnp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { independent_senators = independent_final_senators }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { plsr_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsp_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
					rsdrp_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = psr_coalition
					psr_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { psr_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { lkdp_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
					has_government = market_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rkdp_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { vns_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ep_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nrpr_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
					nsnp_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsnp_senators = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = independent_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independent_senators = 0 }
	}
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = plsr_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsp_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rsdrp_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = psr_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = lkdp_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rkdp_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = vns_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = ep_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nrpr_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsnp_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = independent_senators }
			
	set_variable = { senate_support = temp1 }
}
parties_mp_recalc = {
	plsr_mp_recalc = yes
	nsp_mp_recalc = yes
	rsdrp_mp_recalc = yes
	psr_mp_recalc = yes
	lkdp_mp_recalc = yes
	rkdp_mp_recalc = yes
	vns_mp_recalc = yes
	ep_mp_recalc = yes
	nrpr_mp_recalc = yes
	nsnp_mp_recalc = yes
	independent_mp_recalc = yes
	mp_support_calc = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_total_mp }

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = mp_total }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker > mp_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_mp = temp1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker < mp_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_mp = temp1 }
		}
	}
}
plsr_mp_recalc = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { plsr_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = plsr_mp
		set_variable = { plsr_total_mp = plsr_mp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { plsr_mp = 0 }
	}
}

rsdrp_mp_recalc = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = rsdrp_mp
		set_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp = rsdrp_mp }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = rsdrp_mp
		set_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp = rsdrp_mp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
					rsdrp_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = 0 }
	}
}

	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { lkdp_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = lkdp_mp
		set_variable = { lkdp_total_mp = lkdp_mp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { lkdp_mp = 0 }
	}
}

nsnp_mp_recalc = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSNP_separated
			has_country_flag = nrpr_banned
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
			set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
			divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
			set_variable = { nsnp_mp = temp1 }
			round_variable = nsnp_mp
			set_variable = { nsnp_total_mp = nsnp_mp }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
			set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
			divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
			set_variable = { nsnp_mp = temp1 }
			round_variable = nsnp_mp
			set_variable = { nsnp_total_mp = nrpr_mp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
						nsnp_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { nsnp_mp = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nsnp_total_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { nsnp_mp = 0 }
	}
}
independent_mp_recalc = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_independent_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { independent_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = independent_mp
		set_variable = { independent_total_mp = independent_mp }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_independent_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = mp_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { independent_mp = temp1 }
		round_variable = independent_mp
		set_variable = { independent_total_mp = independent_mp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = independent_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independent_mp = 0 }
	}
}
final_senators_recalc = {
	set_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_total_senators }
	set_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_total_senators }
	
	add_to_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_total_regional_senators }
	
	### Adding presidential senators
	add_to_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_presidential_senators }
	

	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_final_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = senate_total }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker > senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker < senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
	}
}

parties_senators_recalc = {
	plsr_senators_recalc = yes
	nsp_senators_recalc = yes
	rsdrp_senators_recalc = yes
	psr_senators_recalc = yes
	lkdp_senators_recalc = yes
	rkdp_senators_recalc = yes
	vns_senators_recalc = yes
	ep_senators_recalc = yes
	nrpr_senators_recalc = yes
	nsnp_senators_recalc = yes
	independent_senators_recalc = yes
	plsr_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	nsp_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	rsdrp_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	psr_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	lkdp_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	rkdp_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	vns_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	ep_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	nrpr_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	nsnp_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	independent_regional_senators_recalc = yes
	
	final_senators_recalc = yes
	
	senators_support_calc = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_total_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_total_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = senate_total }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker > senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker < senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
	}
}

		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_plsr_percentage_senate_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = senators_election_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { plsr_senators = temp1 }
		round_variable = plsr_senators
		set_variable = { plsr_total_senators = plsr_senators }
	}

		limit = {

					has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition

	}

		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { independent_regional_senators = temp1 }
		round_variable = independent_regional_senators
		set_variable = { independent_total_regional_senators = independent_regional_senators }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = bolsheviks_allowed
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_independent_percentage_vote }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = senators_election_regional_total }
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 100 }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
		set_variable = { independent_regional_senators = temp1 }
		round_variable = independent_regional_senators
		set_variable = { independent_total_regional_senators = independent_regional_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = independent_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independent_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
}

RUS_increase_plsr_pop = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_plsr_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			RUS_state_increase_plsr_pop = yes
		}
	}
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = syndicalist
		popularity = 0.07
	}
}

RUS_state_increase_pop = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_idea = RUS_Maria_A_Spiridonova_hog_rso }
		}
		RUS_state_increase_plsr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_syn
					has_idea = RUS_Sergey_M_Kirov_hog_syn
				}
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_nsp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				psr_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_psr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				rsdrp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_rsdrp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				lkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_lkdp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				rkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_rkdp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				nsnp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_nsnp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				vns_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_vns_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_hog_sco
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_ep_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo
			}
		}
		RUS_state_increase_nrpr_pop = yes
	}	
}
RUS_clamp_all_state_pop = {
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop < RUS_state_pop_check }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = RUS_state_total_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 10 }
		
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop min = 0	max = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop > RUS_state_pop_check }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = RUS_state_total_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 10 }
		
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
		
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
	}
}
RUS_state_increase_plsr_pop = {
	ROOT = { custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_plsr_pop_tt }
	hidden_effect = {
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = 0.035 }
		random_list = {

		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

RUS_state_increase_psr_pop = {
	ROOT = { custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_psr_pop_tt }
	hidden_effect = {
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop = 0.035 }
		random_list = {
			7 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			7 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			7 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			7 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			12 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			15 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			15 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			15 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			15 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
		}
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop < RUS_state_pop_check }
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = RUS_state_total_pop }
			divide_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 10 }
			
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }

			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }

			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }

RUS_state_increase_nsnp_pop = {
	ROOT = { custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_nsnp_pop_tt }
	hidden_effect = {
		add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = 0.035 }
		random_list = {
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			11 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			11 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = -0.035 } }
			13 = { add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = -0.035 } }
		}
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		clamp_variable = { 	var = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop	min = 0	max = 1 }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_state_total_pop = THIS.RUS_state_independent_final_pop }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_pop_check = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {

			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }
			add_to_variable = { THIS.RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_pop_check }

RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = {
	clear_array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
	add_to_array = { RUS_Lower_House_Display = 0 }
	resize_array = { RUS_Lower_House_Display = mp_total }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		set_temp_variable = { temp_index = i }
		add_to_variable = { temp_index = -0.01 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { plsr_total_mp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Lower_House_Display^i = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_nsp_Gui_temp = plsr_total_mp }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsp_Gui_temp = nsp_total_mp }
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Lower_House_Display^i = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_psr_Gui_temp = psr_total_mp }
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Lower_House_Display^i = 3 }

				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_lkdp_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_lkdp_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_lkdp_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 6 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp = vns_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 7 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = vns_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp = ep_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 8 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = vns_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = ep_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp = nsnp_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 9 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = vns_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = ep_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = nsnp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp = nrpr_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = plsr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = nsp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = psr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = rsdrp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = lkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = rkdp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = vns_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = ep_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = nrpr_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = nsnp_final_senators }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp = independent_final_senators }
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_Gui_temp > temp_index }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_Senate_Election_Display^i = 11 }
		}
		
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: SENATE-ELECTION ARRAY LENGHT [?RUS_Senate_Election_Display^num]"
	set_variable = { three_fifth_of_senate = RUS_Senate_Election_Display^num }
	multiply_variable = { three_fifth_of_senate = 3 }
	divide_variable = { three_fifth_of_senate = 5 }
}
RUS_count_senate_elects_president = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = psr_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate = vns_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = ep_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSNP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate = nsnp_final_senators }
	}
	
	### Independent Candidates Vote For Ruling###
	if = {
		limit = {
			plsr_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			nsp_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			rsdrp_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			psr_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			lkdp_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			rkdp_in_power = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Viktor_M_Baydalakov_hog_npo
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	### Socialists Unite ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = votes_for_nsp_candidate }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = votes_for_plsr_candidate }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = votes_for_plsr_candidate }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = votes_for_nsp_candidate }
	}
	### Rightists Vote for liberals ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = votes_for_vns_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = votes_for_vns_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = votes_for_ep_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = votes_for_ep_candidate }
	}
	### Conservatives unite ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate = votes_for_ep_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = votes_for_vns_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate = votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate = votes_for_vns_candidate }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsnp_candidate = votes_for_ep_candidate }
	}
	### PSR chooses their side ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Get_Along_With_NRPR }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Denounce_Savinkovism }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
				check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
				check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
				check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Get_Along_With_NRPR
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Denounce_Savinkovism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
				has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
				has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
				has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = votes_for_psr_candidate }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
				has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
		}
	}
	### Who wins?
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = plsr_wins_president
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = nsp_wins_president
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = psr_wins_president
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = rsdrp_wins_president 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = lkdp_wins_president 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_vns_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = rkdp_wins_president 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_nsnp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = vns_wins_president 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {

			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }

	if = {

predetermine_all_presidential_candidates = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
		}

	}
}
